votes. Democratics are talking about modifying the process.

ago\u003C\u002Fspan\u003E\u003C\u002Fdiv\u003E\n \u003Cdiv\u003EOf all the
issues central to the recall — lockdowns, income inequality, crime — one huge
story has been less prominent: During the pandemic, California paid out more
than $11 billion in fraudulent unemployment claims.\u003C\u002Fdiv\u003E\n
